 agenciyaan bataati hai ki desh or sanstha aarthik rup se kitna majbutarating kii duniya main teen standard and pier, mudies or fich kaa nameek credit reating agency (CRA) dendar kii samay par mooldhan or byaaj bhugtan or difolt kii sambhaavna banaakar lone kaa bhugtan karne kii kshamta ko aankati he
 Credit rating agencies indirectly state how strong the country, institution or person is financially and how much debt is dangerous to it or not
 yani vah kitna karj chukaane kii kshamta rakhata he
 It basically tells investors that a firm has a track record and shows how likely it is to be able to return the money
 is samay reating kii duniya main teen standard and pier, mudies or fich kaa naam he
 They occupy about 95 percent of the market
 haalanki maujuuda samay main bharat main 4 credit reating agenciyaan kaam kar rahi hai
 1
 crisil (crisil)yah bharat kii sabase badi reating agency he, jisamen 65 fisadi se adhik bhartiya bazaar hissedari he
 It is serving the manufacturing, services, financial and SME sectors
 standard and pors ke paas ab crisil main bahumat hissedari he
 CRISIL Rating Agency was established in 1987
 2
 ICRA is a major rating agency backed by Moody's ICRA
 mutual funds, aspataalon, buniyadi dhaanche ke vikaas or nirmaan or real estate companiyon ke liye reating jari karti he
 3
 kear (care)care ore se vittiya sanghathan, rajya sarkarein or nagarpalika sansthaaen or saarvajanik upyogitaaon kii reating kii jaati he
 It is a credit rating agency established in 1993, promoted and supported by IDBI, UTI, Canara Bank and other financial institutions and NBFC
 4
 ONICRA is considered an important rating agency in India
 ONICRA ek nijee reating agency he, jo sonu mirchandani dwaara sthapit kii gai he, yah data kaa vishleshan karti he or vyaktiyon or laghu or madhyam udhyamon (esemai) ke liye reating samaadhaan pradaan karti he
 If we talk about various credit rating agencies at the international level, then at present there are three big names in the rating world
 1
 Standard and Poor: The foundation of this rating agency was laid in 1860 by Henry Poor
 yah sabase puraani agency he
 Today, about 40% of the world's rating business is owned by Standard & Poor and Moody's
 2
 Moody's: Moody's was founded in the year 1909 by a man named John Moody
 3
 Fitch: The third well-known rating agency is Fitch; Which is a shortened form of Standard & Poor and Moody's
 reating or uske mynexa (highest safety): desh, company yaa vyakti nivesh karnaa sabase surakshit or laabhadaayak
 AA (high safety): The country, company or individual has great potential to deliver on their promises
 a (adequate Safety): desh, company yaa vyakti ke paas apane vaadon ko puraa karne kii kshamta par badali vipareet paristhitiyon kaa asar pad saktaa he
 BBB (moderate safety): The ability of a country, company or individual to deliver on its promises but more likely to be affected by adverse economic conditions
 CC: desh, company yaa vyakti vartmaan main bahut kamjor
 d (default): Country, company, or individual failed to return loan
 darasal agar kisi company kii reating, agenciyon dwaara acchhee kar di jaati he to us company ko bazaar se paise udhaar lene main pareshaani nahin hoti he
 Also, due to good image in the market, its stock is seen increasing
 isliye desh, company oe vyakti hameshaa acchhee reating kii khoj main rahete hai
 Why is a rating agency necessary? Since the 1980s, the financial system in the country became more control-free and Indian companies started borrowing more and more loans from global debt markets
